```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Kafka SASL Mechanism Configuration Validation

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that validate SASL mechanism configuration at broker startup: the sasl.enabled.mechanisms validation, the JAAS config presence check, and the mechanism-specific configuration validation (SCRAM, GSSAPI, OAUTHBEARER).

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

```

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## SASL Mechanism Configuration Validation at Broker Startup

The validation is distributed across several files:

### 1. `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` Validation
- **`core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaConfig.scala`** — `saslEnabledMechanisms()` reads enabled mechanisms; `validate()` requires that `sasl.mechanism.inter.broker.protocol` is in `sasl.enabled.mechanisms`
- **`clients/.../network/ChannelBuilders.java`** — `serverChannelBuilder()` iterates over all enabled mechanisms and calls `JaasContext.loadServerContext()` for each
- **`clients/.../authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java`** — constructor validates that enabled mechanisms list is non-empty, and that a callback handler and Subject exist for every mechanism

### 2. JAAS Config Presence Check
- **`clients/.../security/JaasContext.java`** — `loadServerContext()` / `defaultContext()` / `load()`: throws `IllegalArgumentException` if no JAAS entry is found for a mechanism (either via `sasl.jaas.config` property or the static JAAS file under `KafkaServer` / `<listener>.KafkaServer` context names)

### 3. Mechanism-Specific Configuration Validation
- **`clients/.../network/SaslChannelBuilder.java`** — `createServerCallbackHandlers()` dispatches to the correct handler per mechanism (SCRAM → `ScramServerCallbackHandler`, OAUTHBEARER → `OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler`, GSSAPI → `KerberosLogin`)
- **`clients/.../scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java`** — SCRAM handler backed by credential cache
- **`clients/.../oauthbearer/OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler.java`** — Production OAUTHBEARER validator (JWKS endpoint, JWT validator)
- **`clients/.../oauthbearer/internals/unsecured/OAuthBearerUnsecuredVal
... (truncated)

The `validate()` block asserts that `sasl.mechanism.inter.broker.protocol` is contained in `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` when SASL is used for inter-broker communication.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/ChannelBuilders.java`: In `serverChannelBuilder()` and the private `create()` method, the server-side code iterates over each mechanism in `BrokerSecurityConfigs.SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG` and calls `JaasContext.loadServerContext()` for each one, triggering JAAS presence validation.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/authenticator/SaslServerAuthenticator.java`: In its constructor (lines 177-186), it validates that `sasl.enabled.mechanisms` is non-null and non-empty, and that a callback handler and Subject exist for every listed mechanism.\\n\\n**2. JAAS config presence check**\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/JaasContext.java`: The `loadServerContext()` method loads or locates the JAAS configuration for each enabled mechanism. `defaultContext()` throws `IllegalArgumentException` with a descriptive message if neither the listener-scoped context name (e.g., `sasl_plaintext.KafkaServer`) nor the global `KafkaServer` entry is found in the JAAS configuration file. The `load()` method validates that the dynamic `sasl.jaas.config` property contains exactly one login module.\\n\\n**3. Mechanism-specific configuration validation**\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/network/SaslChannelBuilder.java`: `createServerCallbackHandlers()` (lines 317-335) selects the appropriate callback handler per mechanism:\\n  - PLAIN \u2192 `PlainServerCallbackHandler`\\n  - SCRAM-SHA-256 / SCRAM-SHA-512 \u2192 `ScramServerCallbackHandler` (requires `credentialCache`)\\n  - GSSAPI \u2192 falls back to `SaslServerCallbackHandler`; also triggers `KerberosLogin` via `defaultLoginClass()` and adds native GSS credentials\\n  - OAUTHBEARER \u2192 `OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler` (default) or a custom class\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/scram/internals/ScramServerCallbackHandler.java`: Handles SCRAM credential lookup from the broker credential cache.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerValidatorCallbackHandler.java`: The production OAUTHBEARER validator; `configure()` validates JWKS endpoint URL and JWT validator configuration.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/internals/unsecured/OAuthBearerUnsecuredValidatorCallbackHandler.java`: The default (non-production) OAUTHBEARER validator; its `configure()` checks that exactly one non-null JAAS mechanism entry is provided.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/security/oauthbearer/OAuthBearerLoginCallbackHandler.java`: Validates OAUTHBEARER login configuration including token endpoint URL.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/CommonClientConfigs.java`: `postValidateSaslMechanismConfig()` ensures that when `security.protocol` is `SASL_PLAINTEXT` or `SASL_SSL`, the `sasl.mechanism` is non-null and non-empty.\\n\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/internals/BrokerSecurityConfigs.java`: Defines `SASL_ENABLED_MECHANISMS_CONFIG` and related broker security configuration constants used throughout the validation chain.\"\n}\n",
